function end1(actor, npc) 
 if has_alife_info("mil_lukash_dead") and has_alife_info("bar_voronin_dead") then 
  game.start_tutorial("mov_desire_1") 
  return 
 end 
 
 if db.actor:money() >= 50000 and has_alife_info("bar_voronin_dead") then 
  game.start_tutorial("mov_desire_2")  
  return 
 end 
 
 if db.actor:character_reputation() >= 1000 and has_alife_info("bar_voronin_dead")  then 
  game.start_tutorial("mov_desire_3")  
  return 
 end 
 
 if db.actor:character_reputation() <= -1000 and has_alife_info("bar_voronin_dead") then 
  game.start_tutorial("mov_desire_4")  
  return 
 end 
 game.start_tutorial("mov_desire_5") 
end
